### [108] [Reappraisal of the Constraints on Heavy Axion-like Particles from Gamma-Ray Bursts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07297)
*Christopher V. Cappiello,Saurav Das,P. S. Bhupal Dev,Takuya Okawa,Soebur Razzaque*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新评估了重轴子类粒子（ALP）与光子耦合的现有限制，并利用伽马射线暴（GRB）提出了新的约束。作者指出ALP在GRB火球中产生效率通常较低，除非GRB异常高能；同时发现此前被排除的参数空间中，ALP衰变可形成次级火球，将伽马射线重加工为各向同性的X射线，从而可用X射线或MeV伽马射线望远镜间接探测~100 MeV量级ALP。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对重ALP-光子耦合的限制可能过于乐观，且未充分考虑GRB真实物理过程（如ALP产生效率、次级火球形成及辐射重加工），需结合更现实的GRB参数和新物理机制更新约束。

Method: 基于两种GRB火球能量注入模型，计算不同GRB参数下的ALP产生率；修正能量损失限制；分析ALP衰变→双光子→e⁺e⁻对产生的次级火球动力学及其X射线再辐射特征；评估未来X射线/MeV伽马射线望远镜点源灵敏度对ALP参数空间的探测能力。

Result: 1) ALP在典型GRB中产生效率低于先前估计；2) 在先前被luminosity criterion排除的参数区，ALP仍可高效产生并形成次级火球，产生可观测的各向同性X射线辐射；3) 未来X射线（如Athena）和MeV伽马射线（如AMEGO）望远镜有望约束新的ALP质量-耦合参数空间。

Conclusion: 利用GRB次级火球的X射线辐射是一种新颖、互补的重ALP探测途径，拓展了传统能量损失和光变曲线方法的适用范围，为多信使天体物理探针提供了新思路。

Abstract: We reassess existing limits and derive new constraints on heavy axion-like particle (ALP) coupling to photons using gamma-ray bursts (GRBs). ALPs can be produced in the hot dense fireball plasma during the initial stage of GRB outflow, thus potentially disrupting the primary fireball and altering the GRB luminosity. We consider the ALP production rate for various GRB parameters in two different energy injection scenarios of GRB fireball formation, and point out that ALP production is less efficient than previously assumed unless a GRB event is exceptionally energetic. We update the existing energy loss bounds using more realistic GRB parameters. We also point out that in the region of parameter space previously constrained by GRB luminosity criterion, ALP production turns out to be still efficient enough to form a secondary fireball via ALP decay to two photons and their subsequent annihilation to electron-positron pair. This secondary fireball reprocesses the gamma-rays from heavy ALP decay into $X$-rays, emitted isotropically from its surface, thus allowing us to probe $\mathcal{O}(100~\mathrm{MeV})$-scale ALPs indirectly using $X$-ray (or future MeV gamma-ray) telescopes, not necessarily directed toward the GRB jet itself. We show that the future point-source sensitivity of $X$-ray and MeV gamma-ray telescopes may allow us to constrain new ALP parameter space.

</details>


### [109] [Gravitational form factors of the pion in light-front holographic QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07305)

Main category: hep-ph

Abstract: Understanding the internal structure of the pion-particularly the energy-momentum distributions of quarks and gluons and the internal mechanical properties encoded in its gravitational form factors-is a fundamental challenge in quantum chromodynamics (QCD). In this work, we study the gravitational form factors using light-front QCD (LFQCD), combined with the holographic QCD. Our main innovation is the introduction of an effective light-front wave function, with its five-dimensional component obtained from holographic QCD, which is then employed, within the light-front QCD framework, to calculate the pion's gravitational form factors $A(Q^2)$ and $D(Q^2)$ as well as its radius. Our computed pion gravitational form factors show good agreement with lattice QCD results, providing nontrivial support for the viability of our phenomenological model.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入 flavor cuboid 参数化：m₁ = m₀ sinξ, m₂ = m₀ cosξ sinζ, m₃ = m₀ cosξ cosζ；将混合角 θ₁₂、θ₂₃ 分别设为 ξ、ζ，并在其立方极限点（ξ*, ζ*）附近展开。

Result: 得到一个可行的唯象假设，预言中微子为正常但近简并的质量谱及近tribimaximal混合；导出 ξ*−θ₁₂、ζ*−θ₂₃ 与 Δm²₂₁/Δm²₃₁ 之间的可检验关联。

Conclusion: 该 flavor cuboid 框架为理解中微子质量与混合起源提供了新几何视角，其关键关联可作为未来实验验证该模型的决定性判据。

Abstract: Given the latest JUNO implication for normal neutrino mass ordering, we parametrize three neutrino masses in a flavor cuboid: $m^{}_1 = m^{}_0 \sinξ$, $m^{}_2 = m^{}_0 \cosξ\sinζ$ and $m^{}_3 = m^{}_0 \cosξ\cosζ$. We find that this cuboid is able to accommodate both neutrino mass degeneracy and tribimaximal flavor mixing in its cubic limit with $ξ^{}_* = \arctan\left(1/\sqrt{2}\right) \simeq 35.26^\circ$ and $ζ^{}_* = 45^\circ$. Assuming $θ^{}_{12} = ξ$ and $θ^{}_{23} = ζ$ for the two large angles of neutrino oscillations and expanding them around $ξ^{}_*$ and $ζ^{}_*$, we propose a viable ansatz which predicts a normal but nearly degenerate neutrino mass spectrum and a nearly tribimaximal neutrino mixing pattern. Testing the achieved correlation among $ξ^{}_* - θ^{}_{12}$, $ζ^{}_* - θ^{}_{23}$ and $Δm^2_{21}/Δm^2_{31}$ will provide a smoking gun for the validity of this ansatz.

### [112] [Fierz-complete four-quark interactions and the QCD phase diagram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07354)
*Zi-ning Wang,Li-jun Zhou,Chuang Huang,Rui Wen,Shi Yin,Wei-jie Fu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用功能重整化群方法研究了Fierz完备的四夸克相互作用动力学及其对有限温密QCD相图的影响，发现除真空中的π和σ道占主导外，临界端点附近其他道耦合显著增强，进而略微增大相边界曲率并使临界端点向更高重子化学势、更低温度方向移动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解四夸克相互作用在QCD相图特别是临界端点附近的动力学作用，以更准确刻画强相互作用物质的相结构。

Method: 采用功能重整化群（FRG）方法，在有限温度和密度下研究Fierz完备的四夸克相互作用对QCD相图的影响。

Result: 真空下仅π和σ道主导；近临界端点时其他四夸克道耦合显著增强；相比单标量-赝标量道，Fierz完备处理使相边界曲率略增，临界端点移向更高μ_B、更低T。

Conclusion: Fierz完备的四夸克相互作用对临界端点位置和相边界形状有不可忽略的影响，需在QCD相结构研究中予以考虑。

Abstract: The dynamics of Fierz-complete four-quark interactions and its influence on the QCD phase diagram have been investigated within the functional renormalization group approach to QCD at finite temperature and densities. It is found that in the vacuum the pion and sigma channels play the overwhelmingly dominant role, and all the other channels are negligible. However, when it is near the critical end point (CEP), the magnitude of four-quark couplings in other channels increases sizably and they become more and more important. In comparison to the single scalar-pseudoscalar channel of four-quark interactions, the dynamics of Fierz-complete four-quark interactions increases a bit the curvature of the phase boundary, and moves the CEP to location of larger baryon chemical potential and smaller temperature.

### [113] [Dark Neutrons as Dark Matter: Collisions in Halos and Direct Detection from Dark CP Violation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07406)
*Pablo Figueroa,Camilo García-Cely,Giacomo Landini*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有非零拓扑角θ的禁闭规范理论，该角度诱导暗π介子与暗重子之间的CP破坏相互作用，从而产生长程Yukawa势，增强暗物质自相互作用；同时，θ项还诱导暗电偶极矩，显著提升直接探测信号，并可通过时间依赖性识别其CP破坏起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索拓扑角θ在复合暗物质模型中的关键作用，统一解释暗物质自相互作用与直接探测增强现象。

Method: 理论分析：基于禁闭规范理论构建含θ项的暗强子模型，推导暗π介子-重子CP破坏耦合、暗电偶极矩及相应直接探测信号；结合Yukawa势计算自相互作用截面，分析 recoil 能谱与时间调制特征。

Result: θ同时控制暗物质自相互作用强度与直接探测率；暗电偶极矩导致核反冲谱特征及可观测的时间依赖信号；自相互作用与直接探测存在参数关联。

Conclusion: 拓扑角θ是连接暗物质自相互作用与直接探测的关键参数，为自相互作用暗物质提供了自然且可检验的理论实现。

Abstract: We consider confining gauge theories with a non-vanishing topological angle $θ$, which induces CP-violating interactions among dark pions and dark baryons, with dark matter consisting of dark neutrons. The $θ$ term generates scalar pion--baryon couplings analogous to the CP-violating pion--nucleon interactions of QCD. These interactions give rise to an attractive long-range Yukawa potential mediated by the dark pions, whose strength is proportional to $θ$. Since the dark pions are naturally light pseudo-Goldstone bosons, the resulting force can lead to sizable dark matter self-interactions, providing a simple and theoretically motivated realization of the self-interacting dark matter paradigm.
  We also investigate the implications for direct detection in scenarios where the dark sector communicates with the Standard Model through a dark photon portal. The $θ$ term induces dark electric dipole moments proportional to $θ$, which couple directly to the electric fields of nuclei and can substantially enhance direct detection rates. We show how the underlying interactions shape the recoil spectra and discuss the possibility of identifying the CP-violating origin of the signal through its time dependence. Finally, we analyze the interplay between dark matter self-interactions and direct detection signals, showing that both are controlled by the same CP-violating parameter. Our results demonstrate that the topological angle $θ$ can play a central role in determining the phenomenology of composite dark matter.

Abstract: We consider a well-motivated class of scotogenic models (the "T1-2-A" variant), and carry out a comprehensive reassessment of its prospects regarding charged lepton flavour violating (cLFV) observables. Aiming only at explaining neutrino oscillation data and putting forward a viable dark matter candidate, a thorough exploration of the model's parameter space suggests that one can have sizeable rates for cLFV observables, especially in rare muon transitions. We have further considered the role of parity and time-reversal asymmetries for cLFV 3-body decays, $\ell_α^+ \to \ell_β^+ \ell_γ^+ \ell_δ^-$, which can be potentially studied in association with polarised muon and tau decays. Result: SModelS v3.0能较好复现多数ATLAS约束，但存在若干未覆盖的拓扑或效率差异；联合CMS数据与统计组合显著收紧限制；仍存在小部分轻电弱微子参数区域（如压缩谱、低截面情形）未被排除。

Abstract: The ATLAS collaboration has recently performed a vast scan of the phenomenological Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model (pMSSM) with a focus on the electroweak-ino sector, and analysed how their Run 2 searches for electroweak production of supersymmetric (SUSY) particles constrain this dataset. All the SLHA files from the scan as well as the constraints from the eight individual searches considered by ATLAS were made publicly available. We use this material to study how well the ATLAS constraints can be reproduced with SModelS v3.0. Moreover, we explore how the picture changes when also including CMS results, and what can be gained by the statistical combination of analyses. Finally, we discuss the part of parameter space with light electroweak-inos that remains valid despite the stringent LHC limits. Our results underscore the need of a broad, multifaceted approach for maximising sensitivity and closing loopholes in the extensive SUSY parameter space.

### [116] [Single inclusive hadron and jet production in lepton-hadron scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07664)
*Jian-Wei Qiu,Kazuhiro Watanabe*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次在QCD+QED联合因子化框架下计算了轻子-强子散射中大横动量单包容强子和喷注产生过程，引入轻子分布函数（LDFs）并推导其DGLAP演化核，为未来电子-离子对撞机实验提供理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统因子化方法仅考虑QCD，而高精度轻子-强子散射实验（如EIC）需同时处理QCD与QED辐射效应，因此需建立QCD+QED联合因子化框架。

Method: 基于联合QCD+QED因子化，将微分截面分解为红外安全硬系数、轻子分布函数（LDFs）、强子部分子分布函数（PDFs）及碎裂函数（FFs）的卷积；推导包含QCD和QED贡献的DGLAP型演化方程，并构造默认LDFs参数化形式。

Result: 给出了Jefferson Lab和未来电子-离子对撞机（EIC）能量下的单包容强子/喷注产生微分截面的理论预测；提出从未来实验数据中提取非微扰LDFs的策略。

Conclusion: QCD+QED联合因子化是描述高精度轻子-强子散射的关键框架，LDFs作为新分布函数具有普适性，其提取将深化对强子结构与QED辐射效应的理解。

Abstract: We present the first calculation of single inclusive hadron and jet production at large transverse momentum in lepton-hadron scattering in a joint QCD+QED factorization approach. The scattering cross section is factorized into a convolution of infrared-safe hard coefficient functions with universal lepton distribution functions (LDFs) and parton distribution functions (PDFs) of the colliding lepton and hadron, respectively, together with fragmentation functions (FFs) of the observed hadron (or jet). With joint QCD+QED factorization, the DGLAP-type evolution equations for LDFs, PDFs, and FFs necessarily have evolution kernels calculated in both QCD and QED. We derive a default set of LDFs for our calculations and discuss a strategy to extract universal, non-perturbative LDFs from future data. We present our calculations for single inclusive hadron and/or jet production at the energies of Jefferson Lab and the future Electron-Ion Collider.

</details>
